 (define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :conditional-effects)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (adjacent ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
                 (when (= ?dir north) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 south))
                 (when (= ?dir south) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 north))
                 (when (= ?dir east)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 west))
                 (when (= ?dir west)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 east)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (adjacent ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

  (:domain exploration)
  (:objects
    kitchen corridor plain patio wood - location
    north south east west - direction
  )
  (:init
    (at kitchen)

    ;; Adjacent connections (bidirectional)
    (adjacent kitchen corridor north)
    (adjacent corridor kitchen south)
    (adjacent kitchen plain south)
    (adjacent plain kitchen north)
    (adjacent kitchen patio east)
    (adjacent patio kitchen west)
    (adjacent kitchen wood west)
    (adjacent wood kitchen east)

    (door corridor kitchen south)
    (door kitchen plain south)
    (door plain kitchen north)
    (door kitchen patio east)

    (door kitchen wood west)
    (door wood kitchen east)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :conditional-effects)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (adjacent ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
                 (when (= ?dir north) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 south))
                 (when (= ?dir south) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 north))
                 (when (= ?dir east)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 west))
                 (when (= ?dir west)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 east)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (adjacent ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

This is previous problem file:

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :conditional-effects)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (adjacent ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
                 (when (= ?dir north) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 south))
                 (when (= ?dir south) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 north))
                 (when (= ?dir east)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 west))
                 (when (= ?dir west)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 east)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (adjacent ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :conditional-effects)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (adjacent ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
                 (when (= ?dir north) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 south))
                 (when (= ?dir south) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 north))
                 (when (= ?dir east)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 west))
                 (when (= ?dir west)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 east)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (adjacent ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :conditional-effects)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (adjacent ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
                 (when (= ?dir north) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 south))
                 (when (= ?dir south) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 north))
                 (when (= ?dir east)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 west))
                 (when (= ?dir west)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 east)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (adjacent ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :conditional-effects)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (adjacent ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
                 (when (= ?dir north) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 south))
                 (when (= ?dir south) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 north))
                 (when (= ?dir east)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 west))
                 (when (= ?dir west)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 east)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (adjacent ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :conditional-effects)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (adjacent ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
                 (when (= ?dir north) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 south))
                 (when (= ?dir south) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 north))
                 (when (= ?dir east)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 west))
                 (when (= ?dir west)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 east)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (adjacent ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :conditional-effects)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (adjacent ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
                 (when (= ?dir north) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 south))
                 (when (= ?dir south) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 north))
                 (when (= ?dir east)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 west))
                 (when (= ?dir west)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 east)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (adjacent ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :conditional-effects)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (adjacent ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
                 (when (= ?dir north) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 south))
                 (when (= ?dir south) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 north))
                 (when (= ?dir east)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 west))
                 (when (= ?dir west)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 east)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (adjacent ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :conditional-effects)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (adjacent ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
                 (when (= ?dir north) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 south))
                 (when (= ?dir south) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 north))
                 (when (= ?dir east)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 west))
                 (when (= ?dir west)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 east)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (adjacent ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :conditional-effects)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (adjacent ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
                 (when (= ?dir north) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 south))
                 (when (= ?dir south) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 north))
                 (when (= ?dir east)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 west))
                 (when (= ?dir west)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 east)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (adjacent ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :conditional-effects)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (adjacent ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
                 (when (= ?dir north) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 south))
                 (when (= ?dir south) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 north))
                 (when (= ?dir east)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 west))
                 (when (= ?dir west)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 east)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (adjacent ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :conditional-effects)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (adjacent ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - direction ?dir - direction)
    (adjacent ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
                 (when (= ?dir north) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 south))
                 (when (= ?dir south) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 north))
                 (when (= ?dir east)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 west))
                 (when (= ?dir west)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 east)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (adjacent ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :conditional-effects)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (adjacent ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
                 (when (= ?dir north) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 south))
                 (when (= ?dir south) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 north))
                 (when (= ?dir east)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 west))
                 (when (= ?dir west)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 east)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (adjacent ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :conditional-effects)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (adjacent ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
                 (when (= ?dir north) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 south))
                 (when (= ?dir south) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 north))
                 (when (= ?dir east)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 west))
                 (when (= ?dir west)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 east)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (adjacent ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :conditional-effects)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (adjacent ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
                 (when (= ?dir north) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 south))
                 (when (= ?dir south) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 north))
                 (when (= ?dir east)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 west))
                 (when (= ?dir west)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 east)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (adjacent ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :conditional-effects)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (adjacent ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
                 (when (= ?dir north) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 south))
                 (when (= ?dir south) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 north))
                 (when (= ?dir east)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 west))
                 (when (= ?dir west)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 east)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (adjacent ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :conditional-effects)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (adjacent ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
                 (when (= ?dir north) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 south))
                 (when (= ?dir south) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 north))
                 (when (= ?dir east)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 west))
                 (when (= ?dir west)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 east)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (adjacent ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :conditional-effects)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (adjacent ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
                 (when (= ?dir north) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 south))
                 (when (= ?dir south) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 north))
                 (when (= ?dir east)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 west))
                 (when (= ?dir west)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 east)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (adjacent ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :conditional-effects)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (adjacent ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
                 (when (= ?dir north) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 south))
                 (when (= ?dir south) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 north))
                 (when (= ?dir east)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 west))
                 (when (= ?dir west)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 east)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (adjacent ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :conditional-effects)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (adjacent ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
                 (when (= ?dir north) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 south))
                 (when (= ?dir south) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 north))
                 (when (= ?dir east)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 west))
                 (when (= ?dir west)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 east)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (adjacent ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

  (:requirements :strips :typing :conditional-effects)
  (:types location direction)

 (define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :conditional-effects)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (adjacent ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
                 (when (= ?dir north) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 south))
                 (when (= ?dir south) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 north))
                 (when (= ?dir east)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 west))
                 (when (= ?dir west)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 east)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (adjacent ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :conditional-effects)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (adjacent ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
                 (when (= ?dir north) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 south))
                 (when (= ?dir south) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 north))
                 (when (= ?dir east)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 west))
                 (when (= ?dir west)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 east)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (adjacent ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :conditional-effects)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (adjacent ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
                 (when (= ?dir north) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 south))
                 (when (= ?dir south) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 north))
                 (when (= ?dir east)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 west))
                 (when (= ?dir west)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 east)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (adjacent ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

  )

    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)

                 (when (= ?dir north) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 south))

 (define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :conditional-effects)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (adjacent ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
                 (when (= ?dir north) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 south))
                 (when (= ?dir south) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 north))
                 (when (= ?dir east)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 west))
                 (when (= ?dir west)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 east)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (adjacent ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :conditional-effects)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (adjacent ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
                 (when (= ?dir north) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 south))
                 (when (= ?dir south) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 north))
                 (when (= ?dir east)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 west))
                 (when (= ?dir west)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 east)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (adjacent ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :conditional-effects)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (adjacent ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :conditional-effects)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (adjacent ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
                 (when (= ?dir north) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 south))
                 (when (= ?dir south) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 north))
                 (when (= ?dir east)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 west))
                 (when (= ?dir west)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 east)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (adjacent ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :conditional-effects)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (adjacent ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
                 (when (= ?dir north) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 south))
                 (when (= ?dir south) (open ?loc2 ?loc1 north))
                 (when (= ?dir east)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 west))
                 (when (= ?dir west)  (open ?loc2 ?loc1 east)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (adjacent ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)
